puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then pierce with another needle, or a third one if you need it, so that the extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then they should be moved equally from one side to the other in order for them to come out, and the needles should be biting in order to hold, like so is the shape:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if some part remains, then anoint the ball of one of his fingers with oil, and push it into that part, and draw out the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if nothing remains, then put this joint or a higher one, and do this until it all comes out firmly.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot pull back due to the dislocation,
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	then you must wrap it with a cloth, until it all comes out;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	then the cup over the joint of the foot or ankle, and so you must do with the other hand, and to the two feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the head of the child is large and it is tight in the birth canal, or he has acute pain gathered at the top,
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	you must push the spiny spathom between your fingers, and open the head and draw out the water;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you can use the instrument called "almidach", from which the shape comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus, the infant's head is naturally large;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	and then pull out the bones with tongs,
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and if the shoulder pops out and is forced, it should be broken as much as the moisture that is in the wound comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, cut it into pieces as small as you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you must pierce it so that the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is above his feet, then the pull is light, and the direction to the mouth of the wound is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is drawn in the belly or foot, then you must draw it with a cloth wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and open the belly or foot, so that the moisture that is in it runs out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	and if other limbs are affected, and the head remains
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	if he also puts his hand into the wound and draws it out to the mouth of the wound;
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	then he puts in a claw or two, and pulls it out;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	and if the mouth of the wound is narrowed by a hot abscess that has formed there, then one must not work on it,
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	then you must administer moist and fatty things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the patient should be given poultices, and warm water to drink.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can get it to lie still, then administer what we have said for a living child:
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one cannot, then let the body be cut into pieces, and nothing of the afterbirth left behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if he is given what we have said about abscesses that come in the bones;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and bloodletting comes, let it be applied with a constrictive poultice, and other remedies are applied.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly an infant had died, then another was sewn onto her, and the other one died too.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, she got an abscess in her armpit, which swelled so much that it opened, and began to discharge a lot.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the cure, and I thought long and hard, but could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong attractive plaster, and out came a bone, and after a few days some more.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very amazed, for I thought that bellies did not have bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	I examined the wound and found a bone inside, until the woman felt better.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman lived like this for a long time, and then she suddenly died a little bit from the pain;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have not recorded this chapter until now because when the masters find a strange thing, they know how to treat it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	how to reset the dislocation to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Hereafter comes the form of the press, to which one adds the books; and at .2. turns of .2. knees of .2. lines.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, let the horns be more subtle on the restriction, and made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and let the mouth of the post be one digit wide, and the edges of the trees one digit, and one palm and a half long;
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in between the .2. limbs are two adjustments of this same post, which are fastened in one and the other, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	and these two settings are placed in the mouth of the wound to open when you turn the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lightweight, is made of boxwood or ebony, according to the appearance of pincers;
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and has on both sides two settings, as you see, a palm long and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you see the wound opened with all the instrument, then let the woman lie on her back, legs hanging and spread;
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	then put the two parts of the instrument together in the wound, and hold the head of the instrument under between his thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand all along the instrument, just as you did with the tongs according to the amount you want to open the mouth of the wound, until the patient does what he wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all decorated, and they have many similarities; and when the practitioner has prepared them, the action is more rapid and higher in status among people due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair over the instrument until you have prepared it, for their necessity is inexcusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained at childbirth, you should instruct the patient to hold her breath and then make her sneeze with snuff, and hold her hands over her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she vomits, that's fine.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a jar or a covered container and put herbs that can open the mouth of the mother, such as chamomile, anise, fennel, and marsh mallow.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All of these herbs, or any of them, are cooked in water over fire; then put one end of the jar or pot into the mother's mouth, and hold the other end with your hand,
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	and let it fester until the vapors enter the wound; then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	Then remove the pus gently.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment and is not gone, then command the patient to soak her left hand in oil of sesamum or in a poultice of alder, and then put it back into the wound.
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and probe the wound; and when she finds it, she should squeeze it gently and stretch it little by little straight, so that the wound does not hurt during extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	But it must be moved slightly to the right and left, and then pulled; it will come loose and separate.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the wound is narrow, we have described the treatment of sneezing, and smoking with herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it doesn't work with everything we have said, then make sure that you don't try to pull it out;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that whoever is at the mouth of the wound, you tie them to the thigh of the woman, then cleanse her with a four-drug ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	if she can and will, and if not, still, when she farts there comes a bad smell from the stomach and head, and it makes the patient sick.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	So you should use suitable fumigations: some of the ancients have tried fumigation with watercress and dry figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The instrument used to fumigate the woman for retained afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is made of glass like a cane, and one puts the slender end in the woman's womb, and the wide end above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and there is fumigation over the charcoal, and the dye until it is wasted, and start another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born without their fundament being pierced; instead, there is a thin membrane.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, the midwife should pierce that membrane with her finger, without using a spit-tipped needle, and she should be careful not to tear it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then apply a poultice of wet linen soaked in wine and oil, then dress the wound with ointment until it heals.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will heal, insert a wooden peg into the hole and leave it for several days, then remove it when the child wants to move around.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes this stemming comes from a wound or abscess suddenly; so it must be stopped suddenly: then it should be treated as we have said with the wooden peg.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula of the fundament
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from under the anus are nodular and grow larger as they emerge from the anus, or in the space between the two parts.
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	if there is one or multiple fistulas; and when that nodule is old, it opens up, and usually discharges a white fluid or pus.
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and sometimes these fistulas are perforating; and they are caused by what comes out of the anus or is vented when the patient makes a bowel movement, and sometimes they burst out on their own.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if there are fistulas that pierce all the way to the bladder, and halfway down the penis; and they can reach the joint of the thigh, and all the way to the scrotum.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows a fistula that seeps from the anus but does not seep:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you stick your index finger into the anus and insert a fine needle of bronze or iron into the fistula when there is no twistiness.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has twistiness, then insert a slender tent or horsehair, as far as you can feel the tent or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you cannot feel it, and there is no discharge or windiness or pus, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	knowing that it does not pierce, then you can hurry to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula penetrates up to the bladder or the urethra, urine leaks out and cannot be stopped by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced all the way to the hip joint, then the tent will be visible all the way to the location.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is twisting and the pain extends around, then it has moved downward, and medicine will not help nor will poultices;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and for these persian ulcers there is no cure except through labor and the vanity of foolish physicians who interfere.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	For that which is not persian and not old, there is hope of healing through fire, as I have experienced.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and let the patient lie on his back, and lift his legs up to his hips, and have his hips tilted towards his stomach;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a tent of bronze, or of wood if there is any twisting, as far as you know the tent goes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the pain is felt around the anus, you should insert your finger.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	If you feel that the membrane has been pierced, and it is exposed where your finger enters the flesh, then you know that it has burst.and you find that it is soft;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if one does not work on it, it cannot be cured.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One can still cure some, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid for this, one burns the cautery slenderly according to the size of the fistula, as it is said before.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and you insert it hot into the fistula all the way to the anus; and do this two or three times, until you know that the burnt flesh is like the quill of a feather.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	Then treat it with poultices of moist bandages and butter, until the burnt flesh comes off; then treat it with ointment that softens and heals.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If he is thus healed, that is good. If not, he cannot be healed otherwise.
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent goes in and does not pierce all the way to the bottom which is in the foundation, and there is between your finger and the tent a thick covering of flesh or skin, and you see the fistula following the covering of the heart;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if it cuts into the beginning of the fistula, and then fills up again before the tent, and then the cautery afterwards, until it reaches the top of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	and the tent will be delivered, and fall down; then cut away those false flesh-growths which look like a bird's feather, and nothing will remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the pus flows out, and cuts between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or with medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For fire cautery brings together two things: scorching of the flesh and stopping of blood and drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the treatment of tents made wet with butter or crushed substances, until the place oozes and the flesh burns in that place;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with swelling onions in a hot charred state, and the remedies are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes to a point from the fundament, and is removed from the body, put your finger in it and probe it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between them there is the skin or the membrane, or it is ready to pierce, then do not use force but rather follow a path of faith and hope through the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either cauterize it as we have said, or cut it to the bottom, or if you can, put in a tent and cure it as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And do not go too deep, lest you cut the tent that holds the fundament, and cause the evacuations to come out through there.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance you will be healed, or you remove that covering and wash it once it has been cut away from the foundation, either by probing or with another pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then probe the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then examine how to restore the wound and keep the fistula in the part above the foundation: if it is a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes there are fistulas according to this manner: and it is when you put the tent in the fistula, and it is on the side of the foundation under the skin above.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	Take a tent pierced at the tip according to this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And thread a twisted thread through it, and put the tent all the way through the thread into the fistula until it reaches the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it pierces through the margin inside, then pull out the thread from that hole, just as you would put your finger into the hole;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	and draw the head with thread, and bring the two shoulders together, and hold them tightly for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it sometimes, until the threads cut through the skin between the two;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then cure the wound until it is sewn up and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not pierce through, then make it pierce in every way you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not appropriate to cover the wound with a bandage until it is completely healed, as we have said, until it is healthy.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spiny spatomile, from which a fistula is made, is very sharp and pointed on one side;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other part it is not, so that one should not cover it, as you can see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are of two types: they can be inside the anus, like grains of resin, with small and large ones, and they bleed.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	And there can be one or more of them, both inside and at the top of the anus; but those that are outside have less moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	And they bleed a little, or have some yellow water or blood, and their color is like the body's.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those who have them inside the anus is that you should tell the patient to strain until they go into a chamber, so that the anus opens and they come out;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	if you hurry it with tweezers or hold it with your nail then pinch it at the roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the tweezers cannot hold them because of moisture, take it with a piece of cloth or cotton or a piece of camel's hair;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	then pull them out with your fingers, then pinch them, and sprinkle some hot powdered herbs on them that act as a cauterizing agent;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you may cauterize them as described in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other remedies until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundations cannot emerge, then cleanse the patient with a sharp and asperous enema to wash away what is in the foundations, so that it may emerge clearly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	and if the patient strains, and the thread comes out of the anus, then the cure is easy;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should grasp them with your fingernail or tweezers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and so that the incision does not need to be made with iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	If you must perform the suturing in this way: take a twisted thread, and thread it through a needle, then pull the thread so that the needle goes through from one side, and turn both ends of the thread underneath the needle,
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is too wide; and tight the thread firmly, then tie a knot in the thread, and remove the needle, and do likewise with all the others, but leave one to drain the excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place over the wound a damp cloth soaked in rose oil or cerate, and apply it to the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let him defecate, and when he has finished, cleanse the wound with ointment and other remedies until it is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from dryness of the bowels or anus
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is a drying up of fluids in the intestines, and due to a constriction of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine avails not.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	Then you should cut it with a spatule or your nail to the quick, which will not let moisture in.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then clean it until it is sore as it ought to be.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot heal, then restart the scraping more aggressively than before, until it heals and is scraped raw.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	where trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Warts are a small appearance of blisters on the body, and they go very deep.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes the wart shakes, and one feels it as dead because of the trembling, and it comes all over the body, and more on the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the cure is that you take a cane of an goose feather, or a strong vulture feather, and put this cane on the vein, so that the purple circle the vein all around;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand along the whole cane so that you press all around the vein, and put it deeply, and squeeze the vein from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see fit to make a cane of bronze or iron according to this form, and let it be slender underneath and drawn out on top:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	do not pierce it, in order to hold it with the finger, and squeeze it. And if you see fit, cauterize the vein as it is before in the chapter of cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	on the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes an enema is made of silver or brass, or of molten bronze or steel; and sometimes one is made from these small and large instruments, according to the person to whom they are administered.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those who are administered for the treatment of children and who are weak and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the small and large enema is above wide, or the belly is bound according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and it has a slit in the belly, as you can see, and the anus is inside; and it has two slits on one side, and one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and the belly where one puts the medicines is made of a beast's bladder or parchment, and it is pierced all around with small holes,
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and there is a distance of one digit between each hole, then tie into these holes a strong thread of twisted thread in a spiral, and assemble the belly so that it looks like a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread, and then give a enema; and this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	Let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the anus with oil or egg yolk, or similar thing, then insert it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the minister squeezes his two hands together, so that it is all empty, then remove the syringe and leave the patient's legs exposed,
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if the medicine wants to come out, let it go as much as he can; and if he sleeps all night, it is even better.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you cleanse him of stomach sickness, and the medicine rushes out, then cleanse him again until he is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are in the anus or an abscess, then use enemas as gentle as for a baby.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is how to make the gentle enema that will not stretch the skin:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already discussed in the division the cure of wounds; now we will discuss the cures with the hands and with medicine, according to the situation.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and according to what makes them.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The objects that make wounds are by stone impact, and sword and knife cuts, or by spear, staff, arrow, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	Or wounds are made according to the places in the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or head, or leg, or belly, or liver, and similar members;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, because their memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head, and the bone is not broken, one should take care whether it is due to a blow from a stone or similar object, and the skin is still intact but the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you suspect a hot abscess: then make the wound bleed quickly from the cephalic vein itself if there is little blood coming from the wound, and let the bleeding be in the opposite direction to the damaged part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and lessen the patient's consumption of wine and rich foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to bleed, then his food should be reduced, and he should not drink wine or eat meat;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and put a poultice on the wound, if a hot abscess forms, simply wet cotton in rose oil or in wine with styptic.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no hot abscess, put on the wound if it is fresh and bleeding, and has not been moved by the wind: powder which I will describe shortly.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the burn has been moved by the air, put on some ointments until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like that of a sword and similar, and the lips cannot be brought together by sutures, then bring them together by stitches, as I will describe for wounds in the belly, at the ribcage.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed to the bone, and it can be closed, but only with a small piece of skin left attached, then close the wound with medicine, and restore tough skin in place of the missing skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	and instruct the patient to eat coarse foods such as testes, cooked wheat, and similar items.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find pus in the skin, but not reaching to the bone, then scrape away the pus, and then cure it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which does not clot, and it cannot be stopped with medicine, then cut the artery, and if you find it dislodged, then tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	and if this does not help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, the cure is light: you must apply this powder that cauterizes so that the burn has healed.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the manner of the powder is as follows: take incense one part, dragon's blood two parts, quicklime three parts, and ground it finely together,
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply it to the wound, and bind it tightly so that it heals well and joins to the flesh.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	and then tie it well, and leave it untied if it is not swollen; for the medicine is not removed until it has healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes cautery is done with chalk alone when incense and dragon's blood are not available, but the wound is cauterized nonetheless.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the cautery has moved the wound, one should stay in the same place and not move at all, and not put any of this powder on it.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but one should apply some digestive poultices, or barley flour made with water and honey, until the wound heals over.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat other treatments until he is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the fracture comes with the wound, and it is small, then I will extract it with fine tweezers:
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about fractures of the head next.
de la plaie dou col	of a wound on the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound is on the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between it and that of the head, but if the nerve of the neck or artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it's a nerve, there's nothing else to do but leave it alone and not apply anything restrictive, because it hurts the nerves and makes them retreat.Car as ners de l’ome sont si tendus sus li corps que s’il fu entamiez, il ne peut demourer as ses leus naturals;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and put nothing cold on the wound, for the substance of the nerves is cold, and their continuation is with the brain, which is the highest member;Car s’on mit froit sus la plaie, il die oft;
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but for the medicine, as with chalk washed in sweet water, and mixed with rosemary oil, and cooked washed also in sweet water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other soft stones are mined according to this method, and moist ointments.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then cut it and bind it with bands, then heal it until it is healed.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and she has a fever and is full of pus, then pierce her or cut lower down;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if the artery is cut, and bleeding occurs, then stop it, and ligature it, and cauterize it if necessary;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	and if the spine of the throat is cut, or the windpipe, and the conduit is guarded, through which food goes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if it cuts the windpipe on the cane of the throat, and does not touch the throat but puts it back according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then strain it gently, and let it rest for some days, then heal it with ointments that cause shedding until it is healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has made an impression on the bone, then he should;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are bone fragments, then you should draw them all out if you can, and those that you cannot reach, then leave until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and let the dislocation be released and aligned;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, then powder it with the powder I have described.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound, and a fistula forms, then treat it as I have said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of a spear or knife wound
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a deep spear or knife wound, and the patient is not bleeding at all: then know that the wound is mortal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep, and the wound is fresh with all its blood, then do not put powder on it in the first hour, or ligature it for fear of fainting,
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and returns to health, and overcomes the disease;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but I apply an attractive ointment, and bind it .2. times a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you don't have an ointment, put old cotton in the wound to absorb moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and let the patient sleep on the wound for .3. days, or .4., or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if there is no twitching or trembling of the heart, nor a shaking of the limbs.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see these good signs, then you know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat it with poultices and other remedies until it is healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot heal, and there is pus, then you know that there is a fistula; treat it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from an incision of a sword or knife, and it is single, in the front or back, then the treatment of that which is in front;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	if it is large, then stitch it; and if it is small, then powder it, and if it has cut into the bone, and there are fragments in it, then clean the wound, and draw out the foreign bodies if they are loose;
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not loose, then let the wound fester, so that the extractions may be easier;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds in other members is the judgment as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	There are great, medium, and small ruptures of the belly;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	Of the great wound, sometimes the intestine, or the nerve of the intestines, protrudes through which the entrance of air;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and the stitching is more difficult, and sometimes the small wound is worse than the large one;
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because one cannot put the intestines back in if one does not put them back in gradually, bit by bit;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	and because the intestines swell as soon as they feel cold, they close up even more if one does not warm them gradually;
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and because it is useful for the more recent wound, one should reset the intestines to their place first. ii.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that the rupture of the belly occurs in four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the two common sutures occur in the suture of the abdomen,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the sutures of other wounds on the body and two other specific sutures are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	nevertheless, they are more suitable with the suture of the abdomen, and I will describe each one and clarify.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small and nothing of the intestine is protruding,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and if something is dislocated, it can be put back by one of two methods:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm it in such a way:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	soak a sponge or soft cloth in warm water only
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or cook in water with squills and cypress and spice,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and rinse the intestines until they're deflated;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes this wine is constricting, and it is better to drink it for deflation.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling go down, then moisten the intestines with water or a mixture of herbs that have been cooked.
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	For this alleviates the pain in the bowels and allows for easy passage.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot be inserted easily, then make a small cut with the instrument used to remove hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	And the first treatment is more painful than the surgery,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	that one must not cut without great necessity.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument to split it with:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut within the curve and do not cut out, and see here the shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged and the intestines pop out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if he puts it back according to its natural shape in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	then you have the power, because this is possible.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is large and it is in the lower part of the abdomen,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you should have the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and puts his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it is in the part below the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	if he puts his head and his foot higher than the parts below,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and also if the rupture of the belly is in one of the two parts
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	if you put your understanding into this, that the injured part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus one should manage what I say in both great and minor wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For minor wounds, use what you are skilled at,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then have in your hands .i. minister compassionate who touches all the routure to his hand,
et assemble les levres;	and bring together the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common method of suturing,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you should thread a needle or more, depending on the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave about a finger's width from the edge of the wound, and push an needle through it with a strong thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce the .2. heads of the skin with the .2. heads of the syringe,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is underneath the skin inside, as far as you can pierce it from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and join the 2 heads of the syringe with the .4 together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then draw it through a double thread around the needle by .2 parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then bring together the two lips of the wound smoothly,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave a space of two fingers, and he thrusts in another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread as you did for the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and do not cease to do this according to what you need of needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until all of the wound is closed;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and the needles are medium-sized, between thin and thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because thin needles pierce all the way through the skin, and the very thick ones cannot pierce well enough.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	that is why they should be medium-sized;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and needles must not be pushed too deep into the flesh and through the skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	so they do not tear and open the wound before it heals;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then cover the heads of the needles with cloth so that they do not blister the patient while sleeping,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and place wicks or threads on the heads of the needles to keep them in place,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them until the wound is healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of suturing with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it requires only one needle,
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and you shall assemble the two heads of the skin and the two heads of the syphilis together on one needle, having a strong thread in between;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced these heads all four together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then re-insert the needle into the part where you began, in the manner that one sews a cloth.
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and place a distance between each stitch equal to the thickness of a thumbnail;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this sewing affects men,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sewed a wound that one man had on his stomach,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which was caused by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than a palm-width large,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and then of the intestines, well 12 palms wide,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and the wound was in his belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned the intestine to where it had been 24 hours before,
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound healed in 15 days, and I cured him.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged him to have died, and it was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not treat it with ointment, for I was in a place where none could be found, nor any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I put cotton on the wound twice a day, and washed it with water of honey until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	Now I will tell you the two proper methods of suturing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	take the needle, and pierce it through the skin just to the bone inside.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has pierced the cortex straight-on, then insert the tip of the syringe or needle where you pierced the skin.
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and then let it pierce through to the outside of the body from within;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the technique for this sewing is the same as that used by leatherworkers to sew pelts:
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and let the הסיב  of one side go once, and take it back from the other, until the seam is completely stitched.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second way of sewing, which Galen describes properly,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	is such that they bring together the two parts naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and apply one end of the thread to one edge, in such a way:The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	stick a needle or sharp instrument near the eye, and pierce only that spot.
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and leave the two eyes of the tear duct;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle and pierce it from the outside inwards until you reach the inside,
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	as two eyes of the tear duct;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce both sides of the dislocated part, just to the bone inside, with .ii. other pins that are on the other side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and it is the most common way to sew and the best.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen says this word, and some testify,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	that one should sew the belly with .ii. needles, or it has thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one needle must be pushed in from one side, and the other from the other, as those who sew up sores do;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and you should know that when a rupture is in the abdomen,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	if the rupture is more painful than at other places in the abdomen.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is such as the judgment of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and when you find the fresh wound full of blood, as long as the pus has moved,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	then re-insert the intestine and tie it off; then put on the powdered charcoal
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if the pus has moved, then put on some ointment that is available until the wound closes;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and cut off the thread and tie up the sutures and the mastic;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then heal the wound as with the others until it is healed;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	and if you have no medicine, put old cotton on it immediately when it begins to ooze,
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and move it twice a day until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you do not need any other medicine for various conditions when wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound will spread to the principal limbs,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	you should wet a light cloth with tempered oil or rose oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the nails and under the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if there is pain or swelling in the bones, which often occurs,The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if they are enema with red wine, and especially if the constipation reaches the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	and it pierces inside, and you should know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to cure than the small one.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine which is called "young" cannot be cured when it is raw,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it's because of the thinness of the veins that they are, and because of the subtlety of the whole body, and the closeness of its nature to the nerves.

et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	and if it has become green or black, then you must tie off the area that is black so that no blood flow comes from there,

de la routure dou boueil	of the wound where the boil was
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are ruptured, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	one can repair it in some cases,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I saw a man was wounded in the belly with a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became a fistula and discharged fluids and gases;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated the wound according to what I knew, and did not stop treating it until it was healed and the wounds closed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw him bleeding, I doubted that the patient had pain in his belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and there was no harm, but he remained in better condition, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and some experimenters said that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it must be bound in such a way:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take thread from a ram's testicles, then gather the lips of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the tremor has opened the mouth, he puts it against both lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	so that it pulls open his mouth;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then he grasps the head and holds it so that it cannot escape;
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then he puts another tremor after in the same way as before, until the wound is completely seized;
et cout la plaie.	and examine the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If they enter the intestines and cause no harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	one can tie off the intestine with a thin thread cut from the intestine of an animal,
en teil maniere:	in such a way:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the end of this intestine thread which is very charred,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie to the end of this thread a thin, twisted flax thread,
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then thread the needle with the intestine, and sew it up, and then return it to its original place;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this way of stitching is not foreign except according to the path of faith and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	and if the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the internal grails, there is no healing without subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of fistula wherever it may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	You should know that any wound or abscess, when it breaks open, is universally called a "fistula".
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and especially when it is swollen and filled with pus.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the green-colored, tough, white nodulation, where one does not feel pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and is as smooth as the feather of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	and sometimes it is clear and thin, and sometimes thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes it is small, and sometimes large;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	and I have spoken of it in the section on wounds that any wound that is not healed and has no scabs
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	this is only due to one of the seven causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	that is, by the smallness of blood or body;
ou por sa malice;	or because of its wickedness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard charcoal inside, and on the lips, which does not allow blisters to form;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or because there is too much phlegm;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or because the wound is putrid and the matter of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or because the medicine is not good for the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the corruption is a type of pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or because in that region digestion is slow and health comes late, and it swells by nature;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the cures of medicines in the division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Then I shall tell you about the treatment of a fistula which is caused by manual work.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	You should know that a fistula can occur in any part of the body:
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	because they come from large veins, arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or the face, intestines, bladder, or any part of the body,The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	at the spine of the back, or at any joint of the hands or feet;

et estent sus .i. drapeil de lin que cuevre tout le sein;	and they are placed on a linen cloth that covers the entire breast;
puis cope as forces endroit le pertus dou sein .i. poc plus large dou premier,	then press firmly on the opening of the breast a bit larger than the first,
pues estent oignement souef sus .i. autre drapel selonc la quantiteit dou pertus,	then put ointment on another cloth according to the quantity of the opening,
et le met sus le pertus dou sein por aligier la bowe, et n’oster mie le grant drapeil fuers que aprés maint jor une fois;	and place it over the aperture of the breast to ease the bowels, and do not loosen the large cloth until after many days once.
et celui qui est sor le pertus dou sein, oste sovent por oster la bowe,	and that which is over the aperture of the breast, loosen often to ease the bowels,
et saiches ceu que corra de la bowe, se c’est venin ou poc ou assez, ou digeste, ou indigeste;	and know what flows from the bowels, whether it is poison, pus, or enough, or digested, or undigested;
et pren warde se li patiens sent dolor ou nom, et s’il i a aposteme ou non,	and take care if the patient feels pain or not, and if there is an abscess or not,
et quant ta medicine s’est en teil maniere estendue et tu vois la nature que saut sus le pertus dou sein,	and when your medicine has spread in such a way and you see the nature that leaps up from the hole of the breast,
si saiches que li seins s’aert ja, et aproche li santez;	you know that the breast has opened, and approaches the saint.
et puis le deslie le matin, ou le tier jor, et quant tu delies la plaie,	And then loosen it in the morning, or at noon, and when you loosen the wound,
si chainge .i. autre drapeil, et renovele l’oignement.	change to another type of cloth, and renew the ointment.
Et se li seins giete bowe indigeste aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie.	And if breast milk flows crookedly after many days, know that the breast will not heal.
Et se venins subtilz cort aprés lonc tens, si ne te desperer mie de la santeit,	And if subtle poisons flow after a long time, do not despair of health,
car li santez aproche. Car il i a homes cui tarde enjanremens de char en ses plaies, et de ces que font le contraire;	because health is approaching. For there are people who have slow healing in their wounds, and others who heal quickly;
et se bowe indigeste saut dou sein aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie;	and if breast milk flows crookedly after many days, know that the breast will not heal;
et se li seins tarde d’aerdre, et est porloigniez, si ajoste medicines sechans moistes en substance et seches en vertut,	and if the breast is slow to harden, and is distant, then apply medicines that are moist in substance but dry in virtue,
si com oignement diafinit, car il i a grant partie de vitriole, et c’est li derriene medicine;	as an ointment that penetrates, for it contains a large portion of vitriol, and it is the most powerful medicine;
pren oignement dyafinit, et le font avec oile roset, et l’arose de viel vin igal en substance;	take the penetrating ointment, and prepare it with rose oil, and equal parts of old wine;
puis le confit et en use; et ceu meisme fait mielz cuit engroissiez,	then cook it and use it; and with the same, cook honey thickly,
quant oignemens dyafinit n’est presens,	when specific diseases are not present,
ou tu pren mirre et aloen et encens, et le broie, et le poudre sus le miel quant il est sor le feu;	take myrrh, aloe, and incense, grind them up and dust them over honey while it is on the fire;
et puis en glue .i. drapel, et l’estent sor le sein, et aucune fois i aministre on aristologe longe,	and then apply it to a cloth, and place it on the chest, and sometimes administer an arystologus, a long ointment,
et racines de lis celeste, qui est ausi com farine de veces et centoire;	and roots of celestial lily, which is like flour of wheat and centaury;
et en use de simples ou de compostes: broie les, et en fai poudre, et met sus le miel que j’ai dit, et en use;	and use simples or composites: grind them, make them into powder, and put them on the honey I mentioned, and use it;
et se li cure est alongie, et n’est curez par ceste cure,	And if the wound is long, and not healed by this treatment,
adonc saiches que la corruptions est em parfont, et fait empression en l’os, ou as membres durs, ou as liemens;	then you will know that the corruption is deep, and it causes swelling in the bone, or in hard limbs, or in tissues;
si le cure de la cure de fistule, si com nos avons dit ci devant.	if the treatment for a fistula, as we have said before.
de l’aposteme de l’ungle	of the abscess of the nail
Panarice est un aposteme que naist desoz l’ungle dou pouchiet de la main,	Panarice is an abscess that arises underneath the fingernail on the tip of the finger,
ou dou piet, ou par aventure naist en autres dois;	or from the toe, or sometimes it can arise in other places too;
et quant il est envielliez, et on n’i prent garde, si i vient .i. aposteme chaus,	and when it becomes suppurated, and no attention is paid to it, then a hard abscess will form;
et corront et giete bowe tant qu’elle corront la racine de l’ungle, et par aventure la corront toute;	and run and flow low until they reach the root of the nail, and perhaps they will run all the way.
et vient li corrosions jusc’a l’os, tant qu’il i vient dolor puant, et est li chiés dou doi larges, et est li color fuxe.	and the corrosion reaches the bone, causing a foul-smelling pain, and the shoulder is swollen on both sides, and the colour is yellow.
Quant tu le cures si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie,	When you treat it as we have described in the division, and the treatment does not help,
si covient que tu copes a i. fer toute la superfluiteit qui est demoree de l’ungle,	you must cut away all the excess that remains on the nail,
puis cauterize la plaie aprés.	then cauterize the wound after.
